## it's time to deploy

### Scene description

 Low-fi image-based meme idea: Two people, in a room full of computers, panicking and trying to find the right cord to plug in.

### Image prompt

 Two people, panicking, searching for cord to plug in, surrounded by computers, photorealistic, 35mm film, very soft pink undercurrents like aggressive salmon pink ff2a8d, in the style of tame impala innerspeaker
